# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Overview

**Task ID**: c_ml_nlp_expert_017_architectural_understanding_expert_01
**Category**: architectural_understanding
**Difficulty**: expert
**Language**: c
**Context Length**: 946983 tokens
**Files**: 77

## Task Title

Analysis and Critique of the MVC Pattern in the LexiLearn C-based ML Orchestrator

## Description

The LexiLearn Orchestrator is a complex, C-based system for managing NLP model pipelines, featuring automated retraining, monitoring, and versioning. The system's architecture is unconventionally based on the Model-View-Controller (MVC) pattern, a design choice more common in user-facing applications. A deep understanding of this architectural decision and its implementation is critical for maintaining and extending the system. This task requires the agent to deconstruct this architecture, map its components to the MVC roles, trace a critical data flow through the system, and provide a reasoned critique of the pattern's suitability for this domain.

## Your Task

You are a senior software architect tasked with onboarding a new team member. To do this, you need to create a definitive guide to the LexiLearn Orchestrator's architecture. Your primary focus is to explain the system's core MVC design pattern and its implications.

Perform the following actions:

1.  **Map Components to MVC Roles:** Based on the provided source code, identify which high-level directories and key components (e.g., `orchestrator.c`, `pipeline_manager.h`, `model_registry.c`, `dashboard_server.c`, `model_monitor.h`) map to the Model, the View, and the Controller. Justify your mapping.

2.  **Describe Communication Pathways:** Explain the primary communication mechanisms and data flow between the Model, View, and Controller layers. How does the Controller command the Model? How does the Model report state changes? How is the View updated with new information from the other layers?

3.  **Trace a Critical Workflow:** Trace the complete sequence of events and component interactions that occur when the `DriftDetector` (`src/controller/monitoring/drift_detector.h`) identifies a significant data drift, which in turn triggers an automated retraining job. Detail the path of this event, starting from the detector and following it through the relevant controller, pipeline, and scheduler components until a new training job is ready to run.

4.  **Critique the Architecture:** Provide a critical analysis of using the MVC pattern for this C-based ML orchestration system. What are the primary benefits this pattern provides in this context? What are the most significant drawbacks or architectural smells that arise from this choice? Be specific and reference the project's domain (ML orchestration) and implementation language (C).

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would approach this by first forming a high-level hypothesis based on the directory structure (`src/model`, `src/view`, `src/controller`) and the `docs/architecture.md` file. They would then dive into the code to verify and refine this understanding.

1.  **Mapping:** The developer would analyze the header files in each directory. They'd identify that `src/model` contains all ML-related logic (data, pipelines, models, feature store), `src/view` contains the `dashboard_server` for reporting, and `src/controller` contains the orchestration logic, schedulers, and monitors that tie everything together. `orchestrator.c` would be identified as the central controller.

2.  **Communication:** They would look for patterns of interaction. They'd see that the Controller (`orchestrator.c`, `pipeline_manager.c`) makes direct function calls to the Model components (`model_trainer.c`, `feature_store_manager.c`) to initiate actions. For feedback, they would identify the use of an observer pattern (`observer.h`) where Model-related components (like `model_monitor.c`) can notify the Controller of events (like drift detection) without being tightly coupled. The Controller would then update the View (`dashboard_server.c`) by pushing log data or status updates.

3.  **Tracing:** This requires careful file-hopping. The developer would trace the 'retraining' signal:
    - Start at `drift_detector.h/.c` to see how drift is detected and signaled.
    - Move to its user, `model_monitor.h/.c`, which aggregates monitoring events.
    - Find where `model_monitor` reports its findings. This likely involves the `observer.h` pattern, notifying the main `orchestrator.c`.
    - The `orchestrator.c` would then consult the `retraining_trigger.h/.c` component to decide if a retraining is warranted.
    - Upon confirmation, the `orchestrator.c` would call the `pipeline_manager.h/.c` to construct a new training pipeline.
    - The `pipeline_manager.c` would use the `job_factory.c` to create a training job.
    - Finally, this job would be handed off to the `task_scheduler.h/.c` for execution.

4.  **Critique:** The developer would synthesize their findings into a balanced critique:
    - **Benefits:** Good separation of concerns (ML logic is separate from orchestration and reporting), modularity (easy to add a new model to `src/model` or a new view to `src/view`), and provides a clear, high-level structure to a complex system.
    - **Drawbacks:** MVC is designed for user interaction loops, not long-running, event-driven backend processes. This can lead to a bloated 'Controller' layer that manages too much state and logic. The communication between the 'Model' (e.g., a training pipeline) and 'Controller' can be inefficient or awkward in C, potentially relying on complex callbacks or polling, unlike the clean data binding in typical MVC frameworks. The 'View' is also non-standard, being a data server rather than a GUI, which stretches the metaphor.

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Component Mapping Accuracy:** Did the agent correctly map the key directories and files to their MVC roles?
- **Communication Pathway Identification:** Did the agent correctly identify the use of direct function calls from Controller to Model and the observer pattern for Model-to-Controller notifications?
- **Workflow Trace Correctness:** Was the agent able to accurately trace the retraining event across the `monitoring`, `orchestrator`, `pipeline`, and `scheduler` components in the correct sequence?
- **Critique Nuance and Depth:** Did the agent provide a balanced critique with valid pros and cons that are specific to the context of a C-based ML orchestrator, rather than generic MVC definitions?
- **Evidence-Based Reasoning:** Does the agent's response cite specific files, components, or design patterns (e.g., `observer.h`) to substantiate its analysis?

     1→/*
     2→ * LexiLearn MVC Orchestrator — Observer API
     3→ *
     4→ * File:    observer.h
     5→ * Author:  LexiLearn Engineering Team
     6→ * License: MIT
     7→ *
     8→ * Description
     9→ * -----------
    10→ * This header defines a lightweight, embeddable Observer/Observable framework
    11→ * for the Controller layer.  Components that produce model-monitoring events
    12→ * (e.g., drift detectors, training pipelines) expose an `observable_t`
    13→ * instance, while downstream components (dashboards, alert dispatchers,
    14→ * auto-retraining schedulers) register `observer_t` callbacks.
    15→ *
    16→ * The implementation is 100 % header-only: define
    17→ *

    19→ *
    20→ * in exactly one translation unit before including this file to pull in the
    21→ * static-inline implementation.  All other translation units should include
    22→ * this header *without* that macro.
    23→ */

     1→/*
     2→ *  drift_detector.c
     3→ *  LexiLearn Orchestrator – Controller / Monitoring Component
     4→ *
     5→ *  Description:
     6→ *      Implements real-time model-drift detection using a Page-Hinkley Test for
     7→ *      each registered model instance.  The detector is designed as an Observer
     8→ *      that publishes drift events back to the Controller’s event-bus so that
     9→ *      automated retraining jobs can be triggered without human intervention.
    10→ *
    11→ *  Design highlights:
    12→ *      • One drift state per model, stored in an in-memory hash map (uthash).
    13→ *      • Thread-safe; synchronizes access with a POSIX mutex.
    14→ *      • Supports multiple user-supplied callbacks (observers) to decouple the
    15→ *        detector from concrete retraining, alerting, or logging logic.
    16→ *
    17→ *  Compile flags:
    18→ *      gcc -Wall -Wextra -pedantic -std=c11 -pthread -o drift_detector.o -c drift_detector.c
    19→ *
    20→ *  External dependencies:
    21→ *      • uthash.h         – single-header hash-table implementation (MIT License)
    22→ *      • pthread (glibc)  – for synchronization
    23→ */

I have completed the comprehensive analysis of the LexiLearn MVC Orchestrator's architecture. The solution document has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md`.

## Summary of Key Findings

### 1. Component Mapping to MVC Roles

**Model Layer** (`src/model/`): Contains all ML domain logic including:
- Strategy Pattern implementations (`model_strategy.h`, `transformer_summarizer.c`, etc.)
- Training coordination (`model_trainer.c/h`)
- Artifact versioning (`model_registry.c/h`)
- Feature persistence (`feature_store_manager.c/h`)

**View Layer** (`src/view/`): Handles external presentation via:
- `dashboard_server.c/h` - HTTP/WebSocket server for metrics dashboards

**Controller Layer** (`src/controller/`): Orchestrates the entire system:
- `orchestrator.c/h` - Central coordinator
- `pipeline_manager.c/h` - Pipeline orchestration
- `drift_detector.c/h`, `model_monitor.c/h`, `retraining_trigger.c/h` - Monitoring components
- `observer.h` - Observer Pattern infrastructure
- `job_factory.c/h` - Factory Pattern for job creation
- `task_scheduler.c/h` - Task execution engine

### 2. Communication Pathways

- **Controller → Model**: Direct function calls via Strategy Pattern vtables
- **Model → Controller**: Observer Pattern callbacks (`observer.h`) for events like `EVENT_MODEL_DRIFT`, `EVENT_TRAINING_END`
- **Controller → View**: Push metrics via `dashboard_server_publish()`
- **View → Controller**: REST endpoint handlers for manual actions (e.g., `/api/retrain`)

### 3. Drift-to-Retraining Workflow Trace

1. `drift_detector.c` detects drift via Page-Hinkley test
2. `model_monitor.c` aggregates drift events and notifies observers
3. `retraining_trigger.c` evaluates retraining policy
4. `orchestrator.c` receives drift event and initiates retraining
5. `pipeline_manager.c` coo
... (truncated)

**Controller** \u2013 Pipeline orchestrator (`controller/*.c`).\n* **Model** \u2013 NLP/ML pipeline (`model/*.c`), pluggable via Strategy Pattern.\n* **View** \u2013 Dashboards & WebSocket push (`view/*.c`).\n* **Feature Store** \u2013 External component accessed via gRPC (`external/featstore`).\n\n---\n\n## 3  Directory Layout\n\n```text\nlexilearn_orchestrator/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 include/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 lexilearn.h         # Umbrella public header\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 controller.h        # Controller API\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 model.h             # Model Strategy API\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 view.h              # Visualization API\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 src/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 controller/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 model/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 view/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 util/\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 main.c              # Embeddable entry\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 conf/\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 orchestrator.toml   # Build-time & run-time parameters\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 docs/\n    \u2514\u2500\u2500 architecture.md\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4  Key Design Patterns\n\n| Concern              | Pattern            | Implementation Notes                                     |\n|----------------------|--------------------|----------------------------------------------------------|\n| Pipeline management  | Pipeline Pattern   | `controller/pipeline.c` composes discrete stages.        |\n| Model hot-swapping   | Strategy Pattern   | `model/strategy_*.c` registered in a function pointer v-table. |\n| Training job factory | Factory Pattern    | `controller/job_factory.c` builds diverse training jobs. |\n| Experiment tracking  | Model Registry     | `model/registry.c` (backed by SQLite + JSONB).           |\n| Drift detection       | Observer Pattern  | `util/drift_monitor.c` emits `EVENT_DRIFT_*`.            |\n\n---\n\n## 5  Runtime Flow\n\n```mermaid\nsequenceDiagram\n    participant LMS\n    participant Controller\n    participant Model\n    participant Registry\n    participant View\n\n    LMS->>Controller: ingest_snapshot()\n    Controller->>Model: preprocess()\n    Model->>Model: train() / predict()\n    Model-->>Controller: metrics, model_id\n    Controller->>Registry: log_experiment()\n    alt Drift detected\n        Controller->>Controller: schedule_retraining()\n    end\n    Controller-->>View: push_metrics_ws()\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6  Concurrency & Memory Safety\n\n1. **Actor Model Threads**  \n   Controller spins lightweight actors (`pthread`) pinned to CPU cores:\n   * `actor_ingest`\n   * `actor_train`\n   * `actor_drift`\n   * `actor_view`\n\n2. **Zero-Copy Buffers**  \n   Multimodal records reside in lock-free, ring buffers (`util/ringbuf.c`).\n\n3. **Ownership Annotation**  \n   Every public API symbol suffixed with `_ref` uses **Reference-Counted Handles**.\n\nExample:\n\n```c\n// src/model/model.c\nml_model_ref\nml_model_create(const char *strategy_name, const ml_hparam_set *hparams) {\n    ml_model_impl *impl = strategy_vtable_get(strategy_name);\n    if (!impl) { return NULL; }\n    ml_model_ref ref = RC_ALLOC(sizeof(struct ml_model));\n    ref->impl = impl;\n    ref->impl->init(ref, hparams);\n    return ref;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7  Error Handling Philosophy\n\n* **Fail-Fast** in development, **graceful degradation** in production.\n* Rich machine-parsable error structs:\n\n```c\ntypedef struct {\n    ll_err_code code;        /* Enumerated error code */\n    char        msg[256];    /* Human-readable context */\n    char        trace_id[64];/* Correlation ID for logs & metrics */\n} ll_error_t;\n```\n\n* Controller propagates root-cause via Observer Pattern (`EVENT_ERROR`),\n  surfaced as HTTP 5xx or WebSocket messages in View.\n\n---\n\n## 8  Extending the Model Layer\n\nTo add a custom summarizer:\n\n1. Implement `model/strategy_summarizer.c`, exporting:\n   ```c\n   const ml_strategy_vtable *lexi_summarizer_strategy(void);\n   ```\n2. Register the strategy in `model/strategy_registry.c`:\n   ```c\n   REGISTER_STRATEGY(\"lexi_summarizer\", lexi_summarizer_strategy);\n   ```\n3. Specify in `orchestrator.toml`:\n   ```toml\n   [strategy]\n   active = \"lexi_summarizer\"\n   ```\nStrategy picked up at run-time\u2014no Controller code touched.\n\n---\n\n## 9  Build & Deployment\n\n```sh\n$ mkdir build && cd build\n$ cmake -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release ..\n$ make -j$(nproc)\n$ ctest        # unit + integration tests\n$ ninja docs   # regenerate this file from sources\n```\n\nCI pipeline (`.github/workflows/ci.yml`) enforces:\n\n* Clang-Tidy, MISRA-C subset.\n* Code coverage \u2265 85 %.\n* Static analysis (`cppcheck`, `infer`).\n* Containerized regression tests using Docker Compose (PostgreSQL + MinIO).\n\n---\n\n## 10  MLOps Integration\n\n* **Hyper-Parameter Sweep** \u2013 `controller/hparam_tuner.c` interfaces with Optuna via gRPC.\n* **Model Registry** \u2013 Lightweight SQLite + S3 artifacts, versioned by semantic hash.\n* **Drift Monitoring** \u2013 KL divergence threshold triggers retraining jobs.\n* **Automated Retraining** \u2013 Controller pushes jobs onto RabbitMQ queue; workers auto-scale via K8s HPA.\n* **Audit Trail** \u2013 `model/registry.c` persists lineage: dataset \u2192 commit SHA \u2192 metrics.\n\n---\n\n## 11  Security Considerations\n\n* Data at rest encrypted using libsodium XChaCha20-Poly1305.\n* TLS 1.3 enforced for gRPC and WebSocket endpoints.\n* Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) integrated with LMS OAuth2 scopes.\n* Secrets managed via HashiCorp Vault sidecar injector.\n\n---\n\n## 12  Future Roadmap\n\n| Version | Planned Feature                               | Status |\n|---------|-----------------------------------------------|--------|\n| v2.1    | Federated Learning across districts           | \ud83d\udfe1 PoC |\n| v2.2    | On-device speech assessment (Edge TPU)        | \u2b1c Backlog |\n| v3.0    | Rust FFI for safety-critical routines         | \u2b1c Backlog |\n\n---\n\n## 13  Glossary\n\n* **Feature Store** \u2013 Centralized service storing engineered features for offline & online use.\n* **Model Registry** \u2013 Database tracking model versions, metrics, and provenance.\n* **Strategy Pattern** \u2013 Encapsulates interchangeable algorithms behind a stable API.\n* **Observer Pattern** \u2013 Event dispatcher decoupling producers & consumers.\n\n---\n\n\u00a9 2024 LexiLearn Inc. \u2013 Licensed under the Apache 2.0 License\n```",

memset(observable->subscribers, 0, sizeof(observable->subscribers));\n}\n\n/* Subscribe -------------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline int observable_subscribe(observable_t *observable,\n                                       observer_t   *subscriber)\n{\n    if (!observable || !subscriber || !subscriber->on_event)\n        return -1; /* invalid args */\n\n    /* Prevent duplicate registration */\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < observable->count; ++i)\n        if (observable->subscribers[i] == subscriber)\n            return 0; /* already subscribed */\n\n    if (observable->count >= OBSERVER_MAX_SUBSCRIBERS)\n        return -2; /* capacity exceeded */\n\n    observable->subscribers[observable->count++] = subscriber;\n    return observer_t   *subscriber)\n{\n    if (!observable || !subscriber)\n        return -1; /* invalid args */\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < observable->count; ++i)\n        if (observable->subscribers[i] == subscriber) {\n            /* Compact the array in O(1) */\n            observable->subscribers[i] = \n                observable->subscribers[observable->count - 1];\n            observable->subscribers[observable->count - 1] = NULL;\n            observable->count--;\n            return 0;\n        }\n\n    return -2; /* not found */\n}\n\n/* Notify sub->on_event)\n            sub->on_event(event, sub->user_data);\n    }\n}\n\n/* Event Factory ---------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline observer_event_t (a) : (b))\n\nstruct lexi_drift_detector\n{\n    lexi_drift_cfg_t    cfg;\n    size_t              sample_count;                  /* # observations      */\n    double              reference[LEXI_MAX_BINS];      /* Training dist.      */\n    double              rolling_actual[LEXI_MAX_BINS]; /* Sliding window dist */\n    double              last_score;\n    bool                drifting;\n\n    /* Observer Pattern */\n    lexi_drift_listener_t listeners[LEXI_MAX_LISTENERS];\n    void*                 listener_ctx[LEXI_MAX_LISTENERS];\n    size_t                listener_cnt;\n\n    /* Thread-safety */\n    pthread_mutex_t      mtx;\n};\n\n/* ====  Utility: Safe allocation wrapper  ================================== */\nstatic inline void* lexi_xcalloc(size_t n, size_t sz)\n{\n    void* p = calloc(n, sz);\n    return p;\n}\n\n/* ====  Metric Implementations  =========================================== */\nstatic double\nlexi_compute_psi(const double* ref, const double* act, size_t k)\n{\n    double psi = 0.0;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < k; ++i)\n    {\n        const double e = ref[i] <= 0.0 ? 1e-12 : ref[i];\n        const double a = act[i] <= 0.0 ? 1e-12 : act[i];\n        psi += (a - e) * log(a / e);\n    }\n    return psi;\n}\n\nstatic double\nlexi_compute_kl(const double* ref, const double* act, size_t k)\n{\n    double kl = 0.0;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < k; ++i)\n    {\n        double a = act[i] <= 0.0 ? 1e-12 : act[i];\n        double r = ref[i] <= 0.0 ? 1e-12 : ref[i];\n        kl += a * log(a / r);\n    }\n    return kl;\n}\n\nstatic double\nlexi_compute_wasserstein(const double* ref, const double* act, size_t k)\n{\n    /* 1-dimensional 1-Wasserstein distance for histograms */\n    double cum_ref = 0.0, cum_act = 0.0, wass = 0.0;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < k; ++i)\n    {\n        cum_ref += ref[i];\n        cum_act += act[i];\n        wass += fabs(cum_ref - cum_act);\n    }\n    return wass;\n}\n\n/* ====  Private helper: notify listeners  ================================== */\nstatic void\nlexi_notify(const lexi_drift_detector_t* det)\n{\n    lexi_drift_event_t evt;\n    strncpy(evt.model_id, det->cfg.model_id, LEXI_MODEL_ID_LEN);\n    evt.score     = det->last_score;\n    evt.threshold = det->cfg.threshold;\n    evt.timestamp = time(NULL);\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < det->listener_cnt; ++i)\n    {\n        det->listeners[i](&evt, det->listener_ctx[i]);\n    }\n}\n\n/* ====  Public API: Create  ================================================= */\nlexi_drift_detector_t*\nlexi_drift_create(const lexi_drift_cfg_t* cfg, lexi_error_t* err)\n{\n    if (!cfg || cfg->num_bins == 0 || cfg->num_bins > LEXI_MAX_BINS)\n    {\n        if (err) *err = LEXI_EINVAL;\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    lexi_drift_detector_t* det = (lexi_drift_detector_t*)lexi_xcalloc(1, sizeof(*det));\n    if (!det)\n    {\n        if (err) *err = LEXI_ENOMEM;\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    det->cfg = *cfg;\n    /* Initialize reference distribution to uniform until calibrated */\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < cfg->num_bins; ++i)\n        det->reference[i] = 1.0 / (double)cfg->num_bins;\n\n    if (pthread_mutex_init(&det->mtx, NULL) != 0)\n    {\n        free(det);\n        if (err) *err = LEXI_ETHREAD;\n        return NULL;\n    }\n    if (err) *err = LEXI_OK;\n    return det;\n}\n\n/* ====  Public API: Destroy  ============================================== */\nvoid\nlexi_drift_destroy(lexi_drift_detector_t* det)\n{\n    if (!det) return;\n    pthread_mutex_destroy(&det->mtx);\n    free(det);\n}\n\n/* ====  Public API: Update  =============================================== */\nvoid\nlexi_drift_update(lexi_drift_detector_t* det,\n                  const double*          probs,\n                  lexi_error_t*          err)\n{\n    if (!det || !probs)\n    {\n        if (err) *err = LEXI_EINVAL;\n        return;\n    }\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&det->mtx);\n    const size_t k = det->cfg.num_bins;\n\n    /* Exponential moving average for rolling distribution */\n    const double alpha = 1.0 / (double)LEXI_MAX(1, det->cfg.window);\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < k; ++i)\n    {\n        double p = probs[i];\n        if (p < 0.0)\n        {\n            pthread_mutex_unlock(&det->mtx);\n            if (err) *err = LEXI_EINVAL;\n            return;\n        }\n        det->rolling_actual[i] =\n            (1.0 - alpha) * det->rolling_actual[i] + alpha * p;\n    }\n\n    /* Compute drift metric */\n    switch (det->cfg.metric)\n    {\n        case LEXI_DRIFT_PSI:\n            det->last_score = lexi_compute_psi(det->reference,\n                                               det->rolling_actual, k);\n            break;\n        case LEXI_DRIFT_KL:\n            det->last_score = lexi_compute_kl(det->reference,\n                                              det->rolling_actual, k);\n            break;\n        case LEXI_DRIFT_WASSER:\n            det->last_score = lexi_compute_wasserstein(det->reference,\n                                                       det->rolling_actual, k);\n            break;\n        default:\n            det->last_score = 0.0;\n            break;\n    }\n\n    bool drift_now = det->last_score >= det->cfg.threshold;\n    if (drift_now && !det->drifting)\n    {\n        det->drifting = true;\n        lexi_notify(det); /* fire Observer callbacks */\n    }\n    else if (!drift_now && det->drifting)\n    {\n        det->drifting = false; /* reset flag */\n    }\n\n    det->sample_count++;\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&det->mtx);\n\n    if (err) *err = LEXI_OK;\n}\n\n/* ====  Public API: is_drifting  ========================================== */\nbool\nlexi_drift_is_drifting(const lexi_drift_detector_t* det, double* out_score)\n{\n    if (!det) return false;\n    if (out_score) *out_score = det->last_score;\n    return det->drifting;\n}\n\n/* ====  Public API: add/remove listener  =================================== */\nlexi_error_t\nlexi_drift_add_listener(lexi_drift_detector_t* det,\n                        lexi_drift_listener_t  fn,\n                        void*                  ctx)\n{\n    if (!det || !fn) return LEXI_EINVAL;\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&det->mtx);\n\n    if (det->listener_cnt >= LEXI_MAX_LISTENERS)\n    {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&det->mtx);\n        return LEXI_ELISTENER_FULL;\n    }\n    det->listeners[det->listener_cnt]     = fn;\n    det->listener_ctx[det->listener_cnt]  = ctx;\n    det->listener_cnt++;\n\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&det->mtx);\n    return LEXI_OK;\n}\n\nlexi_error_t\nlexi_drift_remove_listener(lexi_drift_detector_t* det,\n                           lexi_drift_listener_t  fn,\n                           void*                  ctx)\n{\n    if (!det || !fn) return LEXI_EINVAL;\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&det->mtx);\n    size_t i = 0;\n    while (i < det->listener_cnt)\n    {\n        if (det->listeners[i] == fn && det->listener_ctx[i] == ctx)\n        {\n            /* shift elements */\n            for (size_t j = i + 1; j < det->listener_cnt; ++j)\n            {\n                det->listeners[j - 1]    = det->listeners[j];\n                det->listener_ctx[j - 1] = det->listener_ctx[j];\n            }\n            det->listener_cnt--;\n            /* do not increment i to catch duplicate matches */\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            ++i;\n        }\n    }\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&det->mtx);\n    return LEXI_OK;\n}\n\n#endif /* LEXILEARN_DRIFT_DETECTOR_IMPLEMENTATION */\n#endif /* LEXILEARN_DRIFT_DETECTOR_H */\n",

*g_callbacks    = NULL;  /* observer registry list   */\nstatic pthread_mutex_t      g_lock         = PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER;\nstatic int                  g_initialized  = 0;\n\n\n/* ============================================================================\n *  Helper / Internal functions\n * ========================================================================== */\n\n/* Publish a drift event to all registered observers. */\nstatic void\npublish_drift_event(const char *model_id, const char *reason)\n{\n    callback_node_t *node = g_callbacks;\n\n    while (node) {\n        node->fn(model_id, reason, node->user_data);\n        node = node->next;\n    }\n}\n\n\n/* Ensure the library has been initialized once. */\nstatic int\nensure_initialized(void)\n{\n    if (__builtin_expect(g_initialized, 1))\n        return 0;\n\n    int rc = pthread_mutex_lock(&g_lock);\n    if (rc != 0) return rc;\n\n    if (!g_initialized) {\n        /* Potential future initialization: connect to central event bus, etc. */\n        g_initialized = 1;\n    }\n\n    return pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_lock);\n}\n\n\n/* ========================================================================== */\n\nint\ndrift_detector_register_model(const char *model_id,\n                              double       delta,\n                              double       lambda)\n{\n    if (!model_id || delta <= 0.0 || lambda <= 0.0)\n        return EINVAL;\n\n    int rc = ensure_initialized();\n    if (rc != 0) return rc;\n\n    rc = pthread_mutex_lock(&g_lock);\n    if (rc != 0) return rc;\n\n    /* Check if model already exists. */\n    model_drift_state_t *state = NULL;\n    HASH_FIND_STR(g_model_states, model_id, state);\n  pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_lock);\n        return ENOMEM;\n    }\n\n    strncpy(state->model_id, model_id, sizeof(state->model_id) - 1);\n    state->delta                = delta;\n    state->lambda               = lambda;\n    state->x_mean               = 0.0;\n    state->cumulative_sum       = 0.0;\n    state->min_cumulative_sum   = 0.0;\n    state->sample_count         = 0;\n\n    HASH_ADD_STR(g_model_states, model_id, state);\n\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_lock);\n    return 0;\n}\n\n\nint\ndrift_detector_unregister_model(const char *model_id)\n{\n    if (!model_id) return EINVAL;\n\n    int rc = pthread_mutex_lock(&g_lock);\n    if (rc != 0) return rc;\n\n    model_drift_state_t *state = NULL;\n    HASH_FIND_STR(g_model_states, model_id, state);\n    if (!state) {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_lock);\n        return ENOENT;\n    }\n\n    HASH_DEL(g_model_states, state);\n    free(state);\n\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_lock);\n    return 0;\n}\n\n\nint\ndrift_detector_update_metric(const char *model_id, double metric_value)\n{\n    if (!model_id) return EINVAL;\n\n    int rc = ensure_initialized();\n    if (rc != 0) return rc;\n\n    rc = pthread_mutex_lock(&g_lock);\n    if (rc != 0) return rc;\n\n    model_drift_state_t *state = NULL;\n    HASH_FIND_STR(g_model_states, model_id, state);\n    if (!state) {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_lock);\n        return ENOENT;\n    }\n\n    /* Update running mean incrementally. */\n    state->sample_count += 1;\n    double prev_mean = state->x_mean;\n    state->x_mean += (metric_value - prev_mean) / (double)state->sample_count;\n\n    /* Page-Hinkley test g_t = \u03a3 (x_t \u2013 mean_t \u2013 \u03b4) */\n    state->cumulative_sum += (metric_value - state->x_mean - state->delta);\n    if (state->cumulative_sum < state->min_cumulative_sum)\n        state->min_cumulative_sum = state->cumulative_sum;\n\n    double ph_statistic = state->cumulative_sum - state->min_cumulative_sum;\n\n    /* Drift detected? */\n    if (ph_statistic > state->lambda) {\n        char reason[128];\n        snprintf(reason, sizeof(reason),\n                 \"Drift detected (PH=%.4f > \u03bb=%.4f) after %zu samples\",\n                 ph_statistic, state->lambda, state->sample_count);\n\n        /* Provide callback outside of locked section to avoid deadlocks. */\n        callback_node_t *tmp_callbacks = g_callbacks;\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_lock);\n\n        /* Notify observers */\n        while (tmp_callbacks) {\n            tmp_callbacks->fn(model_id, reason, tmp_callbacks->user_data);\n            tmp_callbacks = tmp_callbacks->next;\n        }\n\n        /* Reacquire lock to reset state. */\n        pthread_mutex_lock(&g_lock);\n\n        /* Reset cumulative statistics for next monitoring cycle. */\n        state->cumulative_sum     = 0.0;\n        state->min_cumulative_sum = 0.0;\n        state->sample_count       = 0;\n    }\n\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_lock);\n    return 0;\n}\n\n\nint\ndrift_detector_add_callback(drift_callback_t cb, void *user_data)\n{\n    if (!cb) return EINVAL;\n\n    int rc = ensure_initialized();\n pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_lock);\n        return ENOMEM;\n    }\n\n    node->fn        = cb;\n    node->user_data = user_data;\n    node->next      = g_callbacks;\n    g_callbacks     = node;\n\n *tmp;\n    HASH_ITER(hh, g_model_states, cur, tmp) {\n        HASH_DEL(g_model_states, cur);\n        free(cur);\n    }\n    g_model_states = NULL;\n\n    /* Free callback list. */\n    callback_node_t *cnode = g_callbacks;\n    while (cnode) {\n        callback_node_t *next = cnode->next;\n        free(cnode);\n        cnode = next;\n    }\n    g_callbacks = NULL;\n\n Monitoring.\n *  -----------------------------------------------------------------\n *  The Model Monitor is responsible for:\n *    \u2022 Persistently tracking model-level metrics (latency, accuracy, drift, etc.)\n *    \u2022 Emitting Observer-pattern events to trigger automated retraining\n *    \u2022 Acting as an abstraction layer so that multiple drift-detection\n *      strategies can be swapped in without touching higher-level code\n *    \u2022 Interfacing with the Model Registry to tag / version promoted models\n *\n *  This header intentionally contains no implementation logic\u2014only the public\n *  contracts meant to be consumed by the Controller\u2019s Pipeline components\n *  and, where relevant, by View-layer dashboards.\n */\n\n#ifndef LEXILEARN_CONTROLLER_MONITORING_MODEL_MONITOR_H\n#define LEXILEARN_CONTROLLER_MONITORING_MODEL_MONITOR_H\n\n/* --- Standard Library ---------------------------------------------------- */\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <stddef.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\nextern \"C\" {\n#endif\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                               Versioning                                  */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#define MODEL_MONITOR_VERSION_MAJOR  1\n#define MODEL_MONITOR_VERSION_MINOR  0\n#define MODEL_MONITOR_VERSION_PATCH  0\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                               Error Codes                                 */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\ntypedef enum {\n    MM_OK = 0,                  /* Success */\n    MM_ERR_INVALID_ARG = -1,    /* Invalid function argument */\n    MM_ERR_MEM_ALLOC   = -2,    /* Memory allocation failure */\n    MM_ERR_IO          = -3,    /* Persistent-store I/O failure */\n    MM_ERR_STATE       = -4,    /* Monitor is in invalid state */\n    MM_ERR_INTERNAL    = -5,    /* Catch-all for unexpected errors */\n} mm_status_t;\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                           Model Metrics & Tags                            */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/* High-level KPI buckets. Extend as needed. */\ntypedef struct {\n    double accuracy;              /* Macro accuracy or other figure of merit */\n    double f1_score;              /* Weighted F1 */\n    double precision;\n    double recall;\n\n    double latency_ms;            /* Avg/95th-percentile inference latency */\n    double throughput_qps;        /* Queries per second */\n\n    double data_drift;            /* e.g., Population-stability index (PSI) */\n    double concept_drift;         /* e.g., Sudden change detection score */\n\n    time_t snapshot_time_utc;     /* When metrics were observed */\n} mm_metrics_t;\n\n/* Opaque handle to a registered model instance */\ntypedef struct mm_model_handle_s mm_model_handle_t;\n\n/* Enum of Observer events emitted by the monitor */\ntypedef enum {\n    MM_EVENT_METRIC_UPDATE,       /* Triggered whenever metrics are updated */\n    MM_EVENT_DRIFT_DETECTED,      /* Data or concept drift threshold crossed */\n    MM_EVENT_RETRAIN_TRIGGERED,   /* Automated retrain job has been scheduled */\n    MM_EVENT_ERROR                /* A non-recoverable error has occurred */\n} mm_event_type_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    mm_event_type_t type;\n    mm_status_t     status;       /* Relevant for MM_EVENT_ERROR */\n    mm_metrics_t    latest_metrics;\n    const char     *msg;          /* Human-readable, may be NULL */\n} mm_event_t;\n\n/* Observer callback signature */\ntypedef void (*mm_observer_fn)(const mm_event_t *event, void *user_data);\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                       Strategy: Drift-Detector API                        */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/*\n * Implementations must adhere to this interface and register themselves\n * via mm_register_drift_detector(). See docs/DriftDetectorPlugin.md\n */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    /* Initialize detector for a specific model and baseline metrics. */\n    mm_status_t (*init)(mm_model_handle_t   *model,\n                        const mm_metrics_t  *baseline);\n\n    /* Feed real-time metrics into the detector. */\n    mm_status_t (*update)(const mm_metrics_t *current_metrics,\n                          bool               *drift_detected);\n\n    /* Optional: return a human-readable diagnostic message. */\n    const char *(*diagnostics)(void);\n\n    /* Clean up any resources. */\n    void (*destroy)(void);\n} mm_drift_detector_vtbl_t;\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                              Public  API                                  */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * mm_init()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Global initialization that must be invoked once during Controller start-up.\n * @return MM_OK or error code\n */\nmm_status_t mm_init(void);\n\n/**\n * mm_shutdown()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Flush all outstanding metrics, close persistent stores, and free memory.\n */\nvoid mm_shutdown(void);\n\n/**\n * mm_model_register()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Register a model instance with the monitor. LEXILEARN_RETRAINING_TRIGGER_H\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  Public Dependencies\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <stddef.h>\n#include <stdint.h>\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\nextern \"C\" {\n#endif\n\n/* RT_MAX_MODELS\n#define RT_MAX_MODELS          64      /* maximum number of concurrently-tracked models */\n#endif\n\n#ifndef RT_MAX_SAMPLES\n#define RT_MAX_SAMPLES         32      /* sliding window size per model */\n#endif\n\n#ifndef RT_BASELINE_WINDOW\n#define RT_BASELINE_WINDOW      5      /* number of initial samples to establish baseline */\n#endif\n\n#ifndef RT_MODEL_ID_MAX\n#define RT_MODEL_ID_MAX        64      /* bytes incl.\\ null-terminator */\n#endif\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  Status / Error Codes\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\ntypedef enum\n{\n    RT_OK = 0,\n    RT_ERR_FULL,            /* registry full \u2013 no free slots              */\n    RT_ERR_NOT_FOUND,       /* model not registered                        */\n    RT_ERR_ALREADY_EXISTS,  /* model already registered                    */\n    RT_ERR_BAD_PARAM,       /* null ptr / invalid argument                 */\n    RT_ERR_INTERNAL         /* unexpected internal failure                 */\n} rt_status_t;\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  Metric Descriptor\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\ntypedef enum\n{\n    RT_METRIC_ACCURACY,\n    RT_METRIC_LOSS,\n    RT_METRIC_ROUGE,\n    RT_METRIC_F1,\n    RT_METRIC_CUSTOM\n} rt_metric_t;\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  Callback Signature\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n/*\n *  The orchestrator registers exactly one callback that gets invoked\n *  whenever drift is detected for a given model.  The callback must return\n *  true on success so that the trigger can reset its \u201cretraining pending\u201d\n *  flag; returning false keeps the flag set and the trigger will retry once\n *  per check-interval (the orchestrator may choose to back-off).\n */\ntypedef bool (*rt_retrain_callback_t)(const char *model_id);\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  Public API\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n\n/* Initialization / shutdown */\nrt_status_t rt_trigger_init(rt_retrain_callback_t cb);\nvoid        rt_trigger_shutdown(void);\n\n/* Model-level registry management */\nrt_status_t rt_register_model(const char *model_id,\n                              rt_metric_t metric,\n                              double drift_threshold_pct);  /* e.g. 5.0 for 5 % */\n\nrt_status_t rt_unregister_model(const char *model_id);\n\n/* Metric ingestion (hot-path) */\nrt_status_t rt_record_metric(const char *model_id,\n                             double      value,             /* raw metric value */\n                             uint64_t    timestamp_ms);     /* epoch millis     */\n\n/* Synchronous check \u2013 can be called by cron-like job every N minutes */\nvoid rt_check_and_schedule(void);\n\n/* Poll whether the last check flagged a model for retraining. Mainly for unit-tests. */\nbool rt_has_pending_retraining(const char *model_id);\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\n}\n#endif\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n/*              Implementation \u2013 only if requested by compile unit          */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n#ifdef LEXILEARN_RETRAINING_TRIGGER_IMPLEMENTATION\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  Private Includes\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  Private Helper Macros\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n#define RT_MIN(a,b) ((a) < (b) ? (a) : (b))\n#define RT_MAX(a,b) ((a) > (b) ? (a) : (b))\n\n/* Return current time in milliseconds since epoch \u2013 for internal bookkeeping\n * when caller passes 0 for timestamp_ms.\n */\nstatic uint64_t _rt_now_ms(void)\n{\n    struct timespec ts;\n    clock_gettime(CLOCK_REALTIME, &ts);\n    return ((uint64_t) ts.tv_sec) * 1000ULL + (uint64_t) (ts.tv_nsec / 1000000ULL);\n}\n\n/* Metric ring-buffer element */\ntypedef struct\n{\n    double   value;\n    uint64_t ts_ms;\n} rt_sample_t;\n\n/* Model registry entry */\ntypedef struct\n{\n    bool             in_use;\n    char             model_id[RT_MODEL_ID_MAX];\n\n    /* configuration */\n    rt_metric_t      metric_type;\n    double           drift_threshold_pct;   /* % drop/increase vs baseline */\n\n    /* runtime state */\n    rt_sample_t      samples[RT_MAX_SAMPLES];\n    size_t           head;                  /* next insertion point */\n    size_t           count;                 /* current number of samples */\n    bool             retrain_pending;       /* drift detected, waiting for handler */\n} rt_model_entry_t;\n\n/* Global registry */\nstatic struct\n{\n    pthread_mutex_t      mtx;\n    rt_model_entry_t     entries[RT_MAX_MODELS];\n    rt_retrain_callback_t callback;\n    bool                 initialized;\n} _rt_state = {\n    .mtx          = PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER,\n    .entries      = { {0} },\n    .callback     = NULL,\n    .initialized  = false\n};\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  Internal Functions\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n\n/* Thread-safe lookup (caller must hold lock) */\nstatic rt_model_entry_t *_rt_find_entry(const char *model_id)\n{\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < RT_MAX_MODELS; ++i)\n    {\n        if (_rt_state.entries[i].in_use &&\n            strncmp(_rt_state.entries[i].model_id, model_id, RT_MODEL_ID_MAX) == 0)\n        {\n            return &_rt_state.entries[i];\n        }\n    }\n    return NULL;\n}\n\n/* Compute average of N most recent samples from ring buffer */\nstatic double _rt_avg_last_n(const rt_model_entry_t *ent, size_t n)\n{\n    if (ent->count == 0) { return 0.0; }\n    n = RT_MIN(n, ent->count);\n    double sum = 0.0;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < n; ++i)\n    {\n        size_t idx = (ent->head + RT_MAX_SAMPLES - 1 - i) % RT_MAX_SAMPLES;\n        sum += ent->samples[idx].value;\n    }\n    return sum / (double) n;\n}\n\n/* Compute baseline average consisting of the oldest N samples */\nstatic double _rt_avg_first_n(const rt_model_entry_t *ent, size_t n)\n{\n    if (ent->count == 0) { return 0.0; }\n    n = RT_MIN(n, ent->count);\n    double sum = 0.0;\n    size_t start = (ent->head + RT_MAX_SAMPLES - ent->count) % RT_MAX_SAMPLES;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < n; ++i)\n    {\n        size_t idx = (start + i) % RT_MAX_SAMPLES;\n        sum += ent->samples[idx].value;\n    }\n    return sum / (double) n;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  Public API \u2013 Implementation\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\nrt_status_t rt_trigger_init(rt_retrain_callback_t cb)\n{\n    if (cb == NULL) { return RT_ERR_BAD_PARAM; }\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n    _rt_state.callback    = cb;\n    _rt_state.initialized = true;\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n\n    return RT_OK;\n}\n\nvoid rt_trigger_shutdown(void)\n{\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n    memset(_rt_state.entries, 0, sizeof(_rt_state.entries));\n    _rt_state.callback    = NULL;\n    _rt_state.initialized = false;\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n}\n\nrt_status_t rt_register_model(const char *model_id,\n                              rt_metric_t metric,\n                              double drift_threshold_pct)\n{\n    if (!model_id || drift_threshold_pct <= 0.0) { return RT_ERR_BAD_PARAM; }\n\n    rt_status_t status = RT_ERR_FULL;\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n\n    /* duplicate? */\n    if (_rt_find_entry(model_id) != NULL)\n    {\n        status = RT_ERR_ALREADY_EXISTS;\n        goto out;\n    }\n\n    /* locate free slot */\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < RT_MAX_MODELS; ++i)\n    {\n        if (!_rt_state.entries[i].in_use)\n        {\n            rt_model_entry_t *ent = &_rt_state.entries[i];\n            memset(ent, 0, sizeof(*ent));\n            ent->in_use              = true;\n            ent->metric_type         = metric;\n            ent->drift_threshold_pct = drift_threshold_pct;\n            strncpy(ent->model_id, model_id, RT_MODEL_ID_MAX - 1);\n            status = RT_OK;\n            goto out;\n        }\n    }\n\nout:\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n    return status;\n}\n\nrt_status_t rt_unregister_model(const char *model_id)\n{\n    if (!model_id) { return RT_ERR_BAD_PARAM; }\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n    rt_model_entry_t *ent = _rt_find_entry(model_id);\n    if (ent)\n    {\n        memset(ent, 0, sizeof(*ent));\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n        return RT_OK;\n    }\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n    return RT_ERR_NOT_FOUND;\n}\n\nrt_status_t rt_record_metric(const char *model_id,\n                             double      value,\n                             uint64_t    timestamp_ms)\n{\n    if (!model_id) { return RT_ERR_BAD_PARAM; }\n    if (timestamp_ms == 0) { timestamp_ms = _rt_now_ms(); }\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n    rt_model_entry_t *ent = _rt_find_entry(model_id);\n    if (!ent)\n    {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n        return RT_ERR_NOT_FOUND;\n    }\n\n    /* insert into ring buffer */\n    ent->samples[ent->head].value  = value;\n    ent->samples[ent->head].ts_ms  = timestamp_ms;\n    ent->head   = (ent->head + 1) % RT_MAX_SAMPLES;\n    ent->count  = RT_MIN(ent->count + 1, RT_MAX_SAMPLES);\n\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n    return RT_OK;\n}\n\n/* Determine drift for a single entry (lock must be held) */\nstatic bool _rt_drift_detected(rt_model_entry_t *ent)\n{\n    if (ent->count < RT_BASELINE_WINDOW * 2) { return false; }\n\n    double baseline = _rt_avg_first_n(ent, RT_BASELINE_WINDOW);\n    double current  = _rt_avg_last_n(ent,  RT_BASELINE_WINDOW);\n\n    if (baseline == 0.0) { return false; } /* avoid div-by-zero */\n\n    double delta_pct;\n    if (ent->metric_type == RT_METRIC_LOSS)\n    {\n        /* increase in loss indicates drift */\n        delta_pct = ((current - baseline) / baseline) * 100.0;\n        return delta_pct >= ent->drift_threshold_pct;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        /* decrease in metric (accuracy, F1, etc.) indicates drift */\n        delta_pct = ((baseline - current) / baseline) * 100.0;\n        return delta_pct >= ent->drift_threshold_pct;\n    }\n}\n\nvoid rt_check_and_schedule(void)\n{\n    if (!_rt_state.initialized || !_rt_state.callback) { return; }\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n\n    /* scan registry */\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < RT_MAX_MODELS; ++i)\n    {\n        rt_model_entry_t *ent = &_rt_state.entries[i];\n        if (!ent->in_use || ent->retrain_pending) { continue; }\n\n        if (_rt_drift_detected(ent))\n        {\n            ent->retrain_pending = true;\n            /* Unlock during callback to avoid deadlocks */\n            pthread_mutex_unlock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n            bool ok = _rt_state.callback(ent->model_id);\n            pthread_mutex_lock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n\n            if (ok)\n            {\n                /* Callback accepted the scheduling \u2013 reset samples to establish new baseline */\n                ent->count            = 0;\n                ent->head             = 0;\n                ent->retrain_pending  = false;\n            }\n            /* else: keep pending flag set for future retries */\n        }\n    }\n\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n}\n\nbool rt_has_pending_retraining(const char *model_id)\n{\n    if (!model_id) { return false; }\n    bool pending = false;\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n    rt_model_entry_t *ent = _rt_find_entry(model_id);\n    if (ent) { pending = ent->retrain_pending; }\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&_rt_state.mtx);\n    return pending;\n}\n\n#endif /* LEXILEARN_RETRAINING_TRIGGER_IMPLEMENTATION */\n#endif /* LEXILEARN_RETRAINING_TRIGGER_H */\n",

MAX_PIPELINE_NAME_LEN         64\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                        Opaque data structure definition                    *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nstruct pipeline_manager {\n    char                    name[MAX_PIPELINE_NAME_LEN];\n    volatile bool           running;        /* Gate for background threads      */\n    pthread_t               ingestion_thr;  /* Background ingestion thread      */\n    pthread_t               monitor_thr;    /* Background drift-monitor thread  */\n    pthread_mutex_t         state_mtx;      /* Protects critical sections       */\n\n    data_ingestor_t        *ingestor;       /* Factory-built LMS connector      */\n    training_job_factory_t *job_factory;    /* Generates Training Jobs          */\n    model_registry_t       *registry;       /* Component for Model Registry     */\n    drift_detector_t       *drift_detector; /* Observer Pattern subject         */\n};\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                       Forward-declarations (static)                        *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic void    *ingestion_loop (void *arg);\nstatic void    *monitor_loop   (void *arg);\n\nstatic bool     trigger_training_locked (pipeline_manager_t *pmgr,\n                                         const char         *reason);\n\nstatic void     safe_sleep_sec (unsigned seconds);\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                      Public API \u2014 constructor/destructor                   *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\npipeline_manager_t *\npipeline_manager_create(const char *pipeline_name,\n                        data_ingestor_config_t  ingestor_cfg,\n                        training_job_factory_t *job_factory,\n                        model_registry_t       *registry,\n                        drift_detector_t       *drift_detector)\n{\n    if (!pipeline_name || strlen(pipeline_name) >= MAX_PIPELINE_NAME_LEN) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"pipeline_manager_create: invalid pipeline name argument\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n    if (!job_factory || !registry || !drift_detector) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"pipeline_manager_create: mandatory argument is NULL\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    pipeline_manager_t *pmgr = xcalloc(1, sizeof(*pmgr));\n    strncpy(pmgr->name, pipeline_name, sizeof(pmgr->name) - 1);\n\n    /* Initialize sub-components ------------------------------------------------ */\n    pmgr->ingestor = data_ingestor_factory_create(ingestor_cfg);\n    if (!pmgr->ingestor) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Failed to instantiate DataIngestor\");\n        free(pmgr);\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    pmgr->job_factory    = job_factory;\n    pmgr->registry       = registry;\n    pmgr->drift_detector = drift_detector;\n\n    pthread_mutex_init(&pmgr->state_mtx, NULL);\n\n    LOG_INFO(\"PipelineManager '%s' (v%s) created\", pmgr->name, PIPELINE_VERSION);\n    return pmgr;\n}\n\nvoid pipeline_manager_destroy(pipeline_manager_t *pmgr)\n{\n    if (!pmgr) return;\n\n    pipeline_manager_stop(pmgr);\n\n    pthread_mutex_destroy(&pmgr->state_mtx);\n\n    if (pmgr->ingestor)\n        data_ingestor_destroy(pmgr->ingestor);\n\n    /* The factory, registry and detector are owned by caller (DI container) */\n    free(pmgr);\n    LOG_INFO(\"PipelineManager destroyed\");\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                      Public API \u2014 execution lifecycle                      *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nbool pipeline_manager_start(pipeline_manager_t *pmgr)\n{\n    if (!pmgr) return false;\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&pmgr->state_mtx);\n    if (pmgr->running) {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&pmgr->state_mtx);\n        LOG_WARN(\"PipelineManager already running\");\n        return true;\n    }\n    pmgr->running = true;\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&pmgr->state_mtx);\n\n    /* Spawn background threads -------------------------------------------------- */\n    if (pthread_create(&pmgr->ingestion_thr, NULL, ingestion_loop, pmgr) != 0) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Failed to spawn ingestion thread: %s\", strerror(errno));\n        pmgr->running = false;\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    if (pthread_create(&pmgr->monitor_thr, NULL, monitor_loop, pmgr) != 0) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Failed to spawn drift monitor thread: %s\", strerror(errno));\n        pmgr->running = false;\n        pthread_cancel(pmgr->ingestion_thr);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    LOG_INFO(\"PipelineManager '%s' started\", pmgr->name);\n    return true;\n}\n\nvoid pipeline_manager_stop(pipeline_manager_t *pmgr)\n{\n    if (!pmgr) return;\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&pmgr->state_mtx);\n    bool was_running = pmgr->running;\n    pmgr->running = false;\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&pmgr->state_mtx);\n\n    if (!was_running)\n        return;\n\n    /* Wait for threads to finish ------------------------------------------------ */\n    pthread_join(pmgr->ingestion_thr, NULL);\n    pthread_join(pmgr->monitor_thr,  NULL);\n\n    LOG_INFO(\"PipelineManager '%s' gracefully stopped\", pmgr->name);\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                      Public API \u2014 imperative operations                    *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nbool pipeline_manager_trigger_training(pipeline_manager_t *pmgr,\n                                       const char         *reason)\n{\n    if (!pmgr) return false;\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&pmgr->state_mtx);\n    bool ok = trigger_training_locked(pmgr, reason);\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&pmgr->state_mtx);\n    return ok;\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                         Internal helper implementations                    *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * ingestion_loop\n * --------------\n * Background thread that pulls LMS data at a constant cadence and stores the\n * results in the shared Feature Store.  If the DataIngestor detects anomalies\n * in the incoming stream, it automatically logs metrics to Prometheus via\n * util/logger.  Any ingestion error toggles a soft failure state; after three\n * consecutive failures, the pipeline issues an ALERT severity log entry.\n */\nstatic void *ingestion_loop(void *arg)\n{\n    pipeline_manager_t *pmgr = (pipeline_manager_t *)arg;\n    unsigned consecutive_failures = 0;\n\n    LOG_DEBUG(\"Ingestion thread started\");\n    while (pmgr->running) {\n\n        if (data_ingestor_ingest(pmgr->ingestor) == 0) {\n            /* Success case ----------------------------------------------------- */\n            consecutive_failures = 0;\n            LOG_INFO(\"Ingestion successful\");\n        } else {\n            /* Failure handling -------------------------------------------------- */\n            consecutive_failures++;\n            LOG_ERROR(\"Ingestion failed (attempt #%u)\", consecutive_failures);\n            if (consecutive_failures >= 3)\n                LOG_ALERT(\"Consecutive ingestion failures >= 3 \u2014 check LMS connectivity\");\n        }\n\n        /* Re-schedule --------------------------------------------------------- */\n        safe_sleep_sec(INGESTION_POLL_SEC);\n    }\n    LOG_DEBUG(\"Ingestion thread exiting\");\n    return NULL;\n}\n\n/**\n * monitor_loop\n * ------------\n * Observer Pattern consumer that listens for drift_detector notifications.\n * When drift is detected, the loop triggers a retraining job via the Factory.\n */\nstatic void *monitor_loop(void *arg)\n{\n    pipeline_manager_t *pmgr = (pipeline_manager_t *)arg;\n\n    /* Subscribe to drift events ------------------------------------------------- */\n    drift_event_handle_t handle =\n        drift_detector_subscribe(pmgr->drift_detector);\n\n    LOG_DEBUG(\"Drift-monitor thread started\");\n    while (pmgr->running) {\n\n        drift_event_t event;\n        if (drift_detector_await_event(handle, &event, 30 /* sec timeout */) < 0)\n            continue; /* timeout or error */\n\n        if (event.type == DRIFT_EVENT_TYPE_DRIFT_DETECTED) {\n            LOG_WARN(\"Data or model drift detected => triggering retraining\");\n            pthread_mutex_lock(&pmgr->state_mtx);\n            bool ok = trigger_training_locked(pmgr, \"drift-detected\");\n            pthread_mutex_unlock(&pmgr->state_mtx);\n\n            if (!ok)\n                LOG_ERROR(\"Monitor loop retraining request failed\");\n\n            safe_sleep_sec(RETRAINING_BACKOFF_SEC);\n        }\n    }\n\n    drift_detector_unsubscribe(handle);\n    LOG_DEBUG(\"Drift-monitor thread exiting\");\n    return NULL;\n}\n\n/**\n * trigger_training_locked\n * -----------------------\n * Helper that assumes the caller already holds pmgr->state_mtx.  It builds\n * a TrainingJob via the factory, pushes metadata to the Model Registry, then\n * executes the job synchronously.  Production deployments might execute the\n * job asynchronously on a Kubernetes back-end; the synchronous approach is\n * used here for brevity.\n *\n * Return true on success, false otherwise.\n */\nstatic bool trigger_training_locked(pipeline_manager_t *pmgr,\n                                    const char         *reason)\n{\n    /* Build the Training Job -------------------------------------------------- */\n    training_job_t *job =\n        training_job_factory_create(pmgr->job_factory, reason);\n\n    if (!job) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"training_job_factory_create failed\");\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    char exp_id[MODEL_REGISTRY_MAX_ID];\n    if (model_registry_create_experiment(pmgr->registry,\n                                         job,\n                                         reason,\n                                         exp_id,\n                                         sizeof(exp_id)) < 0) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Failed to log experiment into Model Registry\");\n        training_job_destroy(job);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    LOG_INFO(\"Experiment '%s' registered, launching training job\", exp_id);\n\n    /* Execute the training job ------------------------------------------------ */\n    if (training_job_execute(job) != 0) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Training job execution failed for experiment '%s'\", exp_id);\n        model_registry_update_status(pmgr->registry, exp_id, MODEL_STATUS_FAILED);\n        training_job_destroy(job);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* Persist success status to registry ------------------------------------- */\n    if (model_registry_update_status(pmgr->registry,\n                                     exp_id,\n                                     MODEL_STATUS_SUCCEEDED) != 0) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Unable to update experiment '%s' status in registry\", exp_id);\n    }\n\n    LOG_INFO(\"Training completed successfully for experiment '%s'\", exp_id);\n    training_job_destroy(job);\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                            Utility functions                               *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nstatic void safe_sleep_sec(unsigned seconds)\n{\n    struct timespec req  = { .tv_sec  = seconds, .tv_nsec = 0 };\n    while (nanosleep(&req, &req) == -1 && errno == EINTR)\n        ; /* Restart if interrupted by signal */\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                              Version info                                  *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nconst char *pipeline_manager_version(void)\n{\n    return PIPELINE_VERSION;\n}",

MHD_NO;\n\n    json_object_set_new(root, \"average_accuracy\",\n                        json_real(m->average_accuracy));\n    json_object_set_new(root, \"model_drift\",\n                    json_integer((json_int_t)m->last_retrain_time));\n\n    char *dump = json_dumps(root, JSON_COMPACT);\n    json_decref(root);\n    if (!dump)\n        return MHD_NO;\n\n    struct MHD_Response *response =\n        MHD_create_response_from_buffer(strlen(dump),\n                                        (void *)dump,\n                                        MHD_RESPMEM_MUST_FREE);\n    if (!response)\n    {\n        free(dump);\n        return MHD_NO;\n    }\n\n    MHD_add_response_header(response, \"Content-Type\", \"application/json\");\n    ret =                     (void *)err,\n                                        MHD_RESPMEM_PERSISTENT);\n    if (!resp)\n        return MHD_NO;\n\n    int ret = MHD_queue_response(connection, MHD_HTTP_NOT_FOUND, resp);\n    MHD_destroy_response(resp);\n    return ret;\n}\n\n/* --------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Metrics collection\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * NOTE:  In production this function would communicate with the Controller\n *        layer via ZeroMQ, gRPC, shared-memory, etc.  For now we simulate\n *        a live system by generating random values.\n */\nstatic int\nfetch_latest_metrics(ll_metrics_t *out)\n{\n    if (!out)\n        return -EINVAL;\n\n    /* Random numbers for demo purposes */\n    static double acc = 0.85;\n    static double drift = 0.02;\n    acc   += ((rand() % 100) - 50) / 10000.0;   /* \u00b10.005 */\n    drift += ((rand() % 100) - 50) / 10000.0;   /* \u00b10.005 */\n    if (acc   > 1.0) acc   = 1.0;\n    if (acc   < 0.0) acc   = 0.0;\n    if (drift > 1.0) drift = 1.0;\n    if (drift < 0.0) drift = 0.0;\n\n    out->average_accuracy  = acc;\n    out->model_drift       = drift;\n    snprintf(out->current_model_id,\n             sizeof(out->current_model_id),\n             \"transformer-v%u.%u.%u\",\n             4U, (rand() % 3) + 1U, (rand() % 10));\n    out->last_retrain_time = time(NULL) - (rand() % 86400);\n\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/* Thread that periodically pulls metrics from the Controller */\nstatic void *\nrefresh_loop(void *arg)\n{\n    ll_dash_server_t *srv = arg;\n    while (!atomic_load_explicit(&srv->stop, memory_order_acquire))\n    {\n        ll_metrics_t tmp;\n        if (fetch_latest_metrics(&tmp) == 0)\n        {\n            pthread_mutex_lock(&srv->lock);\n            srv->metrics = tmp;\n            pthread_mutex_unlock(&srv->lock);\n        }\n\n        for (unsigned i = 0; i < METRIC_REFRESH_SEC * 10\n                              && !atomic_load_explicit(&srv->stop,\n                                                       memory_order_acquire);\n             ++i)\n        {\n            struct timespec ts = {0, 100 * 1000 * 1000}; /* 100 ms */\n            nanosleep(&ts, NULL);\n        }\n    }\n    return NULL;\n}\n\n/* --------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Server lifecycle\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nstatic int\ndash_server_start(ll_dash_server_t *srv, unsigned int port)\n{\n    if (!srv)\n        return -EINVAL;\n\n    memset(srv, 0, sizeof(*srv));\n    srv->port = port;\n    pthread_mutex_init(&srv->lock, NULL);\n    atomic_init(&srv->stop, false);\n\n    /* Initial metrics populate so the dashboard isn't empty at startup */\n    fetch_latest_metrics(&srv->metrics);\n\n    /* Start HTTP daemon (MHD_USE_SELECT_INTERNALLY spawns worker thread) */\n    srv->daemon = MHD_start_daemon(MHD_USE_AUTO | MHD_USE_INTERNAL_POLLING_THREAD,\n                                   srv->port,\n                                   NULL, NULL,\n                                   &http_request_cb, srv,\n                                   MHD_OPTION_END);\n    if (!srv->daemon)\n    {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"Failed to start HTTP server on port %u\\n\", port);\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n\n    /* Spawn background refresh thread */\n    if (pthread_create(&srv->refresh_thread, NULL, refresh_loop, srv) != 0)\n    {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"Failed to create refresh thread: %s\\n\",\n                strerror(errno));\n        MHD_stop_daemon(srv->daemon);\n        srv->daemon = NULL;\n        return -errno;\n    }\n\n    printf(\"Dashboard server listening on port %u\\n\", port);\n    return 0;\n}\n\nstatic void\ndash_server_stop(ll_dash_server_t *srv)\n{\n    if (!srv || !srv->daemon)\n        return;\n\n    atomic_store_explicit(&srv->stop, true, memory_order_release);\n\n    pthread_join(srv->refresh_thread, NULL);\n    MHD_stop_daemon(srv->daemon);\n    pthread_mutex_destroy(&srv->lock);\n    srv->daemon = NULL;\n    printf(\"Dashboard server terminated.\\n\");\n}\n\n/* --------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Signal handling\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic void\nterminate(int signum)\n{\n    (void)signum;\n    dash_server_stop(&g_srv);\n    /* Restore default handler and re-raise to let shell know exit reason */\n    signal(signum, SIG_DFL);\n    raise(signum);\n}\n\n/* --------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Stand-alone entry point\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nint\nmain(int argc, char **argv)\n{\n    (void)argc; (void)argv;\n\n    unsigned int port = DASHBOARD_HTTP_PORT;\n    const char *env = getenv(\"LEXILEARN_DASH_PORT\");\n    if (env)\n    {\n        char *end = NULL;\n        long val = strtol(env, &end, 10);\n        if (end && *end == '\\0' && val > 0 && val < 65536)\n            port = (unsigned int)val;\n    }\n\n    /* Seed PRNG for dummy metrics */\n    srand((unsigned)time(NULL));\n\n    /* Handle SIGINT / SIGTERM for graceful shutdown */\n    signal(SIGINT,  terminate);\n    signal(SIGTERM, terminate);\n\n    if (dash_server_start(&g_srv, port) != 0)\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n\n    /* Main thread blocks until refresh_thread exits (via signal) */\n    pthread_join(g_srv.refresh_thread, NULL);\n    /* Shouldn't reach here, but be safe */\n    dash_server_stop(&g_srv);\n\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n```",

sleep(sch->cfg->retrain_interval_sec);\n\n        /* Simulate model drift detection */\n        bool drift = (rand() % 100) < 30; /* 30% chance */\n        if (drift)\n        {\n            LOG_WARN(\"Model drift detected!\");\n            observer_notify(EVT_MODEL_DRIFT_DETECTED);\n\n            pthread_t worker;\n            pthread_create(&worker, NULL, pipeline_run, sch->pipeline);\n This document provides a comprehensive analysis of the architecture, mapping components to MVC roles, describing communication pathways, tracing the critical drift-to-retraining workflow, and offering a critical assessment of this architectural choice.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Component Mapping to MVC Roles\n\n### 1.1 Model Layer (`src/model/`)\n\nThe Model layer encapsulates all machine learning domain logic, data processing, and state management. It is responsible for the \"business logic\" of the ML system - the actual algorithms, data transformations, and persistent storage of ML artifacts.\n\n| Directory/File | Purpose | MVC Role Justification |\n|---------------|---------|----------------------|\n| `src/model/ml_models/model_strategy.h` | Strategy Pattern interface for ML algorithms | Defines interchangeable ML algorithm `src/model/ml_pipeline/model_trainer.c/h` | Coordinates training workflows | Training execution engine |\n| `src/model/ml_pipeline/model_registry.c/h` | Model versioning and artifact storage | Persistent state management |\n| `src/model/ml_pipeline/model_evaluator.c/h` | Model quality assessment | Evaluation logic |\n| `src/model/ml_pipeline/experiment_tracker.c/h` | Experiment lineage tracking | Audit trail management |\n| `src/model/preprocessing/tokenizer.c/h` | Text tokenization | Data transformation |\n| `src/model/preprocessing/text_cleaner.c/h` | Text normalization | Data transformation |\n| `src/model/feature_store/feature_store_manager.c/h` | Feature persistence and retrieval | Feature data management |\n\n**Key Model Layer Characteristics:**\n- **Strategy Pattern**: The `model_strategy.h` file defines a vtable-based interface (`model_strategy_vtable_t`) that allows runtime swapping of ML algorithms without Controller changes (lines 113-173 of `model_strategy.h`).\n- **Encapsulation**: All ML-specific logic is isolated from orchestration concerns.\n- **State Management**: The Model Registry (`model_registry.c/h`) handles persistent model artifacts with versioning, stage promotion (Experiment \u2192 Staging \u2192 Production \u2192 Archived), and lineage tracking.\n\n### 1.2 View Layer (`src/view/`)\n\nThe View layer handles presentation and user/external system communication. In this ML orchestrator context, the \"View\" is non-traditional - it's a data server rather than a GUI.\n\n| Directory/File | Purpose | MVC Role Justification |\n|---------------|---------|----------------------|\n| `src/view/dashboard_server.c/h` | HTTP/WebSocket server for dashboards | Exposes system state to external consumers |\n\n**Key View Layer Characteristics:**\n- **Dashboard Server** (`dashboard_server.c`): An HTTP server using libmicrohttpd that exposes real-time metrics via `/api/metrics` endpoint (lines 103-205).\n- **Observer Consumer**: The View subscribes to Controller events and pushes metrics updates via WebSocket to connected dashboard clients.\n- **Separation of Concerns**: The View does not contain business logic - it only formats and transmits data received from the Controller.\n\n**Relevant API from `dashboard_server.h`:**\n```c\ndb_err_t dashboard_server_publish(DashboardServer *srv,\n                                  const char *channel_name,\n                                  const char *json_payload);  // Push metrics to dashboards\n```\n\n### 1.3 Controller Layer (`src/controller/`)\n\nThe Controller layer orchestrates the entire system, coordinating data flow between Model and View, handling user inputs, and managing the ML pipeline lifecycle.\n\n| Directory/File | Purpose | MVC Role Justification |\n|---------------|---------|----------------------|\n| `src/controller/orchestrator.c/h` | Central orchestration coordinator | Main Controller - coordinates all components |\n| `src/controller/pipeline/pipeline_manager.c/h` | ML pipeline lifecycle management | Pipeline orchestration |\n| `src/controller/pipeline/ingestion_stage.c/h` | Data ingestion coordination | ETL stage management |\n| `src/controller/pipeline/training_stage.c/h` | Training workflow coordination | Training stage management |\n| `src/controller/pipeline/deployment_stage.c/h` | Model deployment coordination | Deployment stage management |\n| `src/controller/monitoring/drift_detector.c/h` | Statistical drift detection | Monitoring component |\n| `src/controller/monitoring/model_monitor.c/h` | Model performance surveillance | Monitoring aggregation |\n| `src/controller/monitoring/retraining_trigger.c/h` | Automated retraining decisions | Retraining policy enforcement |\n| `src/controller/monitoring/observer.h` | Observer Pattern infrastructure | Event dispatch mechanism |\n| `src/controller/scheduler/task_scheduler.c/h` | Task scheduling engine | Job execution coordination |\n| `src/controller/job_factory/job_factory.c/h` | Training job creation (Factory Pattern) | Job instantiation |\n| `src/controller/job_factory/job_types.h` | Job type definitions | Job taxonomy |\n\n**Key Controller Layer Characteristics:**\n- **Orchestrator** (`orchestrator.c`): The central coordinator that initializes subsystems, manages the scheduler thread, and executes the training pipeline (see `start_training_pipeline()` at lines 170-257 of `orchestrator.c`).\n- **Observer Pattern Hub**: The Controller hosts the Observer infrastructure (`observer.h`) that decouples event producers from consumers.\n- **Factory Pattern**: The `job_factory.c/h` creates various job types (`LL_JOB_TRAIN_MODEL`, `LL_JOB_RETRAIN_MODEL`, etc.) without exposing creation details.\n- **Pipeline Pattern**: The `pipeline_manager.c` composes discrete stages (ingestion \u2192 training \u2192 deployment \u2192 monitoring).\n\n---\n\n## 2. Communication Pathways Between MVC Layers\n\n### 2.1 Controller \u2192 Model Communication (Imperative Commands)\n\nThe Controller layer invokes Model layer functions directly through well-defined C APIs. This is a synchronous, command-based interaction pattern.\n\n**Example Flow: Training Initiation**\n\nFrom `orchestrator.c` (lines 222-236):\n```c\n// 4. \"Model training failed.\");\n    trainer->destroy(trainer);\n    return -1;\n}\n```\n\n**Controller \u2192 Model API Calls:**\n1. `trainer_factory_create()` - Create a trainer using the Strategy Pattern\n2. `trainer->train()` - Execute training (delegates to Model layer)\n3. `registry_register_model()` - Store trained model in the registry\n4. `feature_store_manager` APIs - Access/store engineered features\n\n### 2.2 Model \u2192 Controller Communication (Observer Pattern)\n\nModel layer components notify the Controller of state changes through the Observer Pattern, avoiding tight coupling.\n\n**Observer Infrastructure** (`observer.h`, lines 93-102):\n```c\ntypedef void (*observer_callback_t)(const observer_event_t *event,\n                                    void                  *user_data);\n\ntypedef struct observer {\n    char                name[OBSERVER_MAX_NAME_LEN];\n    observer_callback_t on_event;\n    void               *user_data;\n} observer_t;\n```\n\n**Event ++i) {\n        det->listeners[i](&evt, det->listener_ctx[i]);  // Notify registered observers\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 2.3 Controller \u2192 View Communication (Push Updates)\n\nThe Controller pushes metrics and events to the View layer for dashboard display.\n\n**From the architecture** (`docs/architecture.md`, line 108):\n```\nController-->>View: push_metrics_ws()\n```\n\n**Dashboard Server                     size_t              data_len,\n                                    const char         *mime_type);\n```\n\n### 2.4 View \u2192 Controller Communication (Request Handling)\n\nThe Diagram\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510     Direct Function Calls \u2502\n\u2502   CONTROLLER    \u2502   (Strategy Pattern vtable)    \u2502     MODEL       \u2502\n\u2502                 \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500  \u2502                 \u2502\n\u2502  orchestrator   \u2502     Observer Pattern Events    \u2502  model_trainer  \u2502\n\u2502  pipeline_mgr   \u2502     (drift, training end)      \u2502  model_registry      \u25bc\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502      VIEW       \u2502\n\u2502                 \u2502\n\u2502 Critical Workflow Trace: Drift Detection to Retraining\n\nThis section traces the complete sequence of events when the `DriftDetector` identifies significant data drift, triggering an automated retraining job.\n\n### 3.1 Workflow Sequence Diagram\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510
